#netmonster: <jasonmay> starting out
#netmonster: <Sartak> I prefer a layered interface more than anything, using bottom-up design
#netmonster: <Sartak> see TAEB::World::Monster :)
#netmonster: <Sartak> two layers: one to check whether the monster is a specific type, and another to check general properties about the monster (is it a foe? can I fight it in melee?)

#netmonster: <Sartak> yeah
#netmonster: <Sartak> it doesn't really help to use subclasses for this, because the monster's hostility changes or may not even be known

#netmonster: <toft_> so for example when you're spawning a child

#netmonster: <toft_> you want to block sigchld for a while so you don't miss your child quitting
#netmonster: <toft_> otherwise you'd end up with zombie processes
#netmonster: <toft_> but anyway
#netmonster: <toft_> apache fucks it up hardcore
#netmonster: <toft_> so you end up with processes that don't respond to sigterm
#netmonster: <toft_> or sigalrm, incidentally

#netmonster: <jasonmay> Sartak: so then what do you mean by super dispatchers?
#netmonster: <jasonmay> I certainly hope act 3 isn't the last act
#netmonster: <arcanehl> is
#netmonster: <Sartak> jasonmay: okay. well, let's assume you wanted to use this for your MUD framework
#netmonster: <Sartak> you would have a dispatcher in your MUD framework
#netmonster: <Sartak> which handles things like "quit"
#netmonster: <Sartak> and you would have a dispatcher for the MUD itself
#netmonster: <Sartak> which handles things like "kill arcanehl"
#netmonster: <arcanehl> a commonly needed to be done task
#netmonster: <Sartak> Jifty::Dispatcher can't do this, because it only looks for dispatcher rules in a single class and that's it
#netmonster: <Sartak> Path::Dispatcher supports this, because the MUD itself can say "on 404, use this other dispatcher"
#netmonster: <Sartak> and if your AberMUD::Dispatcher does "use MUD::Dispatcher -base" that relationship is set up for you automaticall
#netmonster: <Sartak> we need this to have a layered dispatcher for Prophet and SD
#netmonster: <jasonmay> ah
